  * grade_story_100.txt (grade=7.4)
    The enchanted orchard with living statues creates a distinctive, visually compelling setting that effectively supports the dreamlike atmosphere. The moon paths and ethereal transformations provide strong sensory elements that enhance the magical tone. However, the world-building lacks specific sensory details beyond the visual, missing opportunities to fully immerse readers through sound, smell, and texture.

  * grade_story_103.txt (grade=5.6)

The jagged reef adds danger to the setting but isn't fully integrated into the narrative.
